Just be sure to fold the bonnet neatly and compactly.<br /><br />There are two settings buttons - speed and temp. This provides four possible combinations...low/cool, low/warm, high/cool, high/warm.<br /><br />I often use large clips to secure my curls while drying. The bonnet fits over these clips and has plenty of room - will work well for larger rollers. It works fine over loose unclipped/unrolled hair as well. I generally use the low/cool setting. When I use the high setting, the bonnet does shift from the air pressure, but will stay in place if I actually tie the strings instead of just pulling them tight - or if I just lightly hold it in place.<br /><br />On the warm setting, the hose gets hot, but it is not uncomfortable and it might be nice in the winter to have the warm hose on my arm. :) The hose connects to the bonnet a little higher up so it does not rest on my neck at all. I have no problem with burning on the neck regardless of temp setting on dryer.   536. I may be jumping the gun slightly by offering up a review after only three uses of the product (maybe I should wait and see how the dryer holds up after a few months or a year), but I was so pleased with the results I thought I'd give one anyway.<br /><br />This baby does the job. I have very long (waist length), thick and coarse hair that I always set in twists or braids after washing. I used to let my hair air-dry, and the natural drying process could take days before I could take the set down if the weather was inhospitable. Now, when I wash and braid or twist my hair and pop on the dryer, my hair is dry after only 45 minutes. It's a miracle!<br /><br />The unit is very well constructed. It comes in a durable plastic case which houses the drying mechanism, and the dryer nozzle, bonnet and plug have their own tidy compartments. The nozzle attaches to the bonnet very easily and securely, and the bonnet itself is very thick but flexible. I'm not sure what the material itself is -- maybe some kind of thermal heat resistant silica.<br /><br />There are two temperatures and two speeds, so you have four drying options. The hottest and highest setting doesn't strike me as being especially hot -- some other reviewers have found the hot setting uncomfortably hot, so it might just be my particular unit that doesn't heat up to the level that others do. I'm very comfortable with the level of heat that I get, though. It dries effectively and I'm confident that my hair won't be damaged.<br /><br />I have a very big head, so the bonnet size is perfect for me. It ties up snugly and I don't feel any air escaping from anywhere it shouldn't once the bonnet is secure (there are ventilation holes throughout the bonnet). The drawstrings tie the bonnet very tightly, and they are very long, so someone with a smaller head than mine might be able to loop the strings around and tie it around the top to make sure it holds in place if they are unsure that the bonnet will hold.<br/><br />The bonnet can be slightly awkward to put on if you have very long hair and are drying it loose. It took a bit of maneuvering to get all of my braids/twists into the bonnet without any of them peeking out, but I eventually found a method and it's not a problem now.<br /><br />The hose attaches at the base of the bonnet, and even though some other reviewers have had a problem with the hot hose touching their necks and backs while it was in use, I have found that the ballooning of the bonnet once turned on causes the hose to stand away from my body and not touch me at all. Maybe the product was re-engineered after the earlier reviews.<br /><br />The dryer can be a bit loud, but not as loud (I don't think) as a standard hair dryer. I'm not distracted by it.<br /><br />All-in-all, I am as happy with this bonnet dryer as I think I could ever be about any bonnet dryer. It's comfortable, drys my hair quickly and safely and it was totally reasonably priced.

I don't know one that isn't though.<br /><br />Other features- Very compact, stands upright easily on a firm surface, and the cord storage cover is able to be closed during use allowing for convenient use and storage.
